 &lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&amp;#xA0;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;Amounts
 for other taxes
 rents
 and research and development costs are not
 presented because each of such amounts is less than 1% of total
 revenues.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;


 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;&lt;font style=TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline&gt;
 Self-Insurance&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;The
 Company is self-insured for certain casualty losses relating to
 automobile liability
 general liability
 workers&amp;#x2019;
 compensation
 property losses
 and medical claims.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;The
 Company also has stop loss coverage to limit the exposure arising
 from these claims.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;Automobile liability
 general
 liability
 workers&amp;#x2019; compensation
 and property losses costs
 are covered by letters of credit with the company&amp;#x2019;s claim
 administrators.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;Due
 to the complexity of estimating the timing and amounts of insurance
 claims
 the Company uses a third-party actuary to estimate the
 casualty insurance obligations on an annual basis.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;In
 determining the ultimate loss and reserve requirements
 the
 third-party uses various actuarial assumptions including
 compensation trends
 health care cost trends
 and discount rates.
 The third-party actuary also uses historical information for claims
 frequency and severity in order to establish loss development
 factors. The actuarial calculation includes a factor to account for
 changes in inflation
 health care costs
 compensation
 and
 litigation cost trends
 as well as estimated future incurred
 claims.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;Large fluctuations in claims can have a
 significant impact on selling
 general and administrative
 expenses.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;


 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=left&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;&lt;font style=TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline&gt;
 NOTE 8 &amp;#x2013; EMPLOYEE BENEFIT PLANS&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;The
 Company has a trusteed &amp;#x201C;Qualified Profit-Sharing Plan&amp;#x201D;
 that was amended and restated effective September 1
 2010
 known as
 the Golden Flake Snack Foods
 Inc. 401(k) Retirement Savings Plan
 (the &amp;#x201C;Plan&amp;#x201D;).&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;Prior to September 1
 2010
 the Plan was named the Golden Flake Snack Foods
 Inc. 401(k) Salary
 Reduction Plan.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;The Plan&amp;#x2019;s trustee was changed
 from New York Life Trust Company to State Street Bank and Trust
 Company effective September 1
 2010.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;Also
 the Company
 appointed Diversified Investment Advisors to provide recordkeeping
 and general administrative services for the Plan effective
 September 1
 2010.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;The
 Company&amp;#x2019;s contributions to the Plan are reviewed and approved
 by the Board of Directors.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;For the year ended June 3
 2011
 the Board approved an increase in the Company match from 20%
 of an employee&amp;#x2019;s eligible contributions to 25% of an
 employee&amp;#x2019;s eligible contributions.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;The
 Company&amp;#x2019;s 401(k) and Profit Sharing Plan changed to December
 31&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top; DISPLAY: inline&gt;st&lt;/font&gt;
 from May 31&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top; DISPLAY: inline&gt;st&lt;/font&gt;
 starting in 2014.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;Total plan contributions for the years
 ended May 29
 2015 and May 30
 2014 were $150
586 and $90
956
 respectively.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;The
 Company has a salary continuation plan with certain of its key
 officers whereby monthly benefits will be paid for a period of
 fifteen years following retirement.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;The Company is
 accruing the present value of all retirement benefits until the key
 officers reach normal retirement age at which time the principal
 portion of the retirement benefits paid are applied to the
 liability previously accrued.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;The change in the
 liability for the Salary Continuation Plan is as
 follows:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;&lt;font style=TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline&gt;
 Nature of the Business&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;The
 Company manufactures and distributes a full line of snack items
 that are sold through its own sales organization and independent
 distributors to commercial establishments that sell food products
 primarily in the Southeastern United States.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

  
  

 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=left&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;&lt;font style=TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline&gt;
 NOTE 5 - LINE OF CREDIT&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 &lt;div style=MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt align=justify&gt;&lt;font style=FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline&gt;The
 Company has a line-of-credit agreement with a local Birmingham bank
 that permits borrowing up to $3 million.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;The
 line-of-credit is subject to the Company&amp;#x2019;s continued credit
 worthiness and compliance with the terms and conditions of the loan
 agreement.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;In October 2014
 the line-of-credit was
 renewed with no changes from the previous year.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;The
 Company&amp;#x2019;s line-of-credit debt at May 29
 2015 was $2
823
477
 with an interest rate of 3.25%
 leaving the Company with $176
523
 of credit availability.&amp;#xA0;&amp;#xA0;The Company&amp;#x2019;s
 line-of-credit debt at May 31
 2014 was $2
528
511 with an interest
 rate of 3.25%
 leaving the Company with $471
489 of credit
 availability.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

Total number of common shares of an entity that have been sold or granted to shareholders (includes common shares that were issued
 repurchased and remain in the treasury). These shares represent capital invested by the firm's shareholders and owners
 and may be all or only a portion of the number of shares authorized. Shares issued include shares outstanding and shares held in the treasury.
